<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;8.01. Other Events. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">On October&#160;29, 2025, Armada Acquisition Corp. II, a Cayman Islands exempted company (&#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">SPAC</span>&#8221;), issued a press release announcing that the ticker symbols for its Class&#160;A ordinary shares, units and public warrants will change from &#8220;AACI,&#8221; &#8220;AACIU&#8221; and &#8220;AACIW,&#8221; to &#8220;XRPN,&#8221; &#8220;XRPNU&#8221; and &#8220;XRPNW,&#8221; respectively. The changes are in connection with the previously announced Business Combination Agreement, entered into on October&#160;19, 2025, by and among SPAC, Pathfinder Digital Assets LLC (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Company</span>&#8221;), Evernorth Holdings Inc. (&#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Pubco</span>&#8221;) and the other parties thereto (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Business Combination Agreement</span>&#8221;). The ticker symbol changes will take place at the opening of trading on The Nasdaq Global Market on Thursday, October&#160;30, 2025. The completion of the business combination (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Business Combination</span>&#8221;) contemplated by the Business Combination Agreement remains subject to shareholder approval and other customary closing conditions, and is expected to close in the first quarter of 2026. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Additional Information and Where to Find It </span></p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">SPAC and Pubco intend to file with the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">SEC</span>&#8221;) a Registration Statement on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">S-4</span> (as may be amended, the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Registration Statement</span>&#8221;), which will include a preliminary proxy statement of SPAC and a prospectus of Pubco (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Proxy Statement/Prospectus</span>&#8221;) in connection with the Business Combination, the private placements of securities in connection with the Business Combination (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Private Placement Transactions</span>&#8221;) and the other transactions contemplated by the Business Combination Agreement and/or as described in this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> (together with the Business Combination and the Private Placement Transactions, the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Proposed Transactions</span>&#8221;). The definitive proxy statement and other relevant documents will be mailed to shareholders of SPAC as of the record date to be established for voting on the Business Combination and other matters as described in the Proxy Statement/Prospectus. SPAC and/or Pubco will also file other documents regarding the Proposed Transactions with the SEC. This Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> does not contain all of the information that should be considered concerning the Proposed Transactions and is not intended to form the basis of any investment decision or any other decision in respect of the Proposed Transactions. BEFORE MAKING ANY VOTING OR INVESTMENT DECISION, SHAREHOLDERS OF SPAC AND OTHER INTERESTED PARTIES ARE URGED TO READ, WHEN AVAILABLE, THE PRELIMINARY PROXY STATEMENT/PROSPECTUS, AND AMENDMENTS THERETO, AND THE DEFINITIVE PROXY STATEMENT/PROSPECTUS AND ALL OTHER RELEVANT DOCUMENTS FILED OR THAT WILL BE FILED WITH THE SEC IN CONNECTION WITH SPAC&#8217;S SOLICITATION OF PROXIES FOR THE EXTRAORDINARY GENERAL MEETING OF ITS SHAREHOLDERS TO BE HELD TO APPROVE THE PROPOSED TRANSACTIONS AND OTHER MATTERS AS DESCRIBED IN THE PROXY STATEMENT/PROSPECTUS BECAUSE THESE DOCUMENTS WILL CONTAIN IMPORTANT INFORMATION ABOUT SPAC, COMPANY, PUBCO AND THE PROPOSED TRANSACTIONS. Investors and security holders will also be able to obtain copies of the Registration Statement and the Proxy Statement/Prospectus and all other documents filed or TO be filed with the SEC by SPAC and Pubco, without charge, once available, on the SEC&#8217;s website at www.sec.gov or by directing a request to: Armada Acquisition Corp. II, 382 NE 191<sup style="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">st</sup> St., Suite 52895, Miami, Florida 33179-3899; email: finance@arringtoncapital.com, or to: Evernorth Holdings Inc., 600 Battery St., San Francisco, California 94111, email: finance@evernorth.xyz. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">NEITHER THE SEC NOR ANY STATE SECURITIES REGULATORY AGENCY HAS APPROVED OR DISAPPROVED THE PROPOSED TRANSACTIONS DESCRIBED HEREIN, PASSED UPON THE MERITS OR FAIRNESS OF THE BUSINESS COMBINATION OR ANY RELATED TRANSACTIONS OR PASSED UPON THE ADEQUACY OR ACCURACY OF THE DISCLOSURE IN THIS REPORT. ANY REPRESENTATION TO THE CONTRARY CONSTITUTES A CRIMINAL OFFENSE. </p>

<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">The securities to be issued by Pubco and the units to be issued by the Company, in each case, in connection with the Proposed Transactions, have not been registered under the Securities Act and may not be offered or sold in the United States absent registration or an applicable exemption from the registration requirements of the Securities Act. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Participants in the Solicitation </span></p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">SPAC, Pubco, Company and their respective directors and executive officers may be deemed under SEC rules to be participants in the solicitation of proxies from SPAC&#8217;s shareholders in connection with the Business Combination. A list of the names of such directors and executive officers, and information regarding their interests in the Business Combination and their ownership of SPAC&#8217;s securities is, or will be, contained in SPAC&#8217;s filings with the SEC. Additional information regarding the interests of the persons who may, under SEC rules, be deemed participants in the solicitation of proxies from SPAC&#8217;s shareholders in connection with the Business Combination, including the names and interests of Company and Pubco&#8217;s directors and executive officers, will be set forth in the Proxy Statement/Prospectus, which is expected to be filed by SPAC and Pubco with the SEC. Investors and security holders may obtain free copies of these documents as described above. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">No Offer or Solicitation </span></p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">This Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> is for informational purposes only and is not a proxy statement or solicitation of a proxy, consent or authorization with respect to any securities or in respect of the Proposed Transactions and shall not constitute an offer to sell or exchange, or a solicitation of an offer to buy or exchange the securities of SPAC, the Company or Pubco, or any commodity or instrument or related derivative, nor shall there be any sale of any such securities in any state or jurisdiction in which such offer, solicitation, sale or exchange would be unlawful prior to registration or qualification under the securities laws of any such state or jurisdiction. No offer of securities shall be made except by means of a prospectus meeting the requirements of the Securities Act or an exemption therefrom. Investors should consult with their counsel as to the applicable requirements for a purchaser to avail itself of any exemption under the Securities Act. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Forward-Looking Statements </span></p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">This Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> contains certain forward-looking statements within the meaning of the U.S. federal securities laws with respect to the Proposed Transactions and the parties thereto. All statements contained in this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> other than statements of historical fact, including, without limitation, statements regarding the Business Combination between SPAC and Pubco; the anticipated benefits and timing of the transaction; the anticipated benefits and timing of the ticker symbol change; expected trading of the combined company&#8217;s securities on Nasdaq; the completion of investments from certain institutional investors; the expected amount of gross proceeds from the Private Placement Transactions; the anticipated use of proceeds from such Private Placement Transactions; the building of the world&#8217;s leading institutional XRP treasury; the amount of XRP expected to be held by the combined company; the combined company&#8217;s future financial performance, the ability of the combined company to execute its business strategy, its market opportunity and positioning; expectations regarding institutional and retail adoption of XRP and participation in DeFi yield strategies; the combined company&#8217;s contributions to the growth and maturity of the ecosystem, using an approach designed to generate returns for shareholders, supporting XRP&#8217;s utility and adoption, alignment with the growth of the XRP ecosystem, and becoming the leading institutional vehicle for XRP; management ensuring operational independence, taking XRP&#8217;s presence in capital markets to the next level, and other statements regarding management&#8217;s intentions, beliefs, or expectations with respect to the combined company&#8217;s future performance, are forward-looking statements. </p>

<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">Forward-looking statements are often identified by the use of words such as &#8220;anticipate,&#8221; &#8220;believe,&#8221; &#8220;continue,&#8221; &#8220;could,&#8221; &#8220;estimate,&#8221; &#8220;expect,&#8221; &#8220;intend,&#8221; &#8220;may,&#8221; &#8220;might,&#8221; &#8220;plan,&#8221; &#8220;potential,&#8221; &#8220;predict,&#8221; &#8220;project,&#8221; &#8220;should,&#8221; &#8220;will,&#8221; &#8220;would,&#8221; and similar expressions, but the absence of these words does not mean that a statement is not forward-looking. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">These forward-looking statements are based on the current expectations and assumptions of SPAC and Pubco and are subject to risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from those expressed or implied by such forward-looking statements. Such risks and uncertainties include, but are not limited to: (1)&#160;the occurrence of any event, change or other circumstances that could delay or prevent the consummation of the proposed Business Combination; (2)&#160;the outcome of any legal proceedings that may be instituted against SPAC, Pubco, the combined company, or others following the announcement of the Proposed Transactions; (3)&#160;the inability to complete the Business Combination due to failure to obtain shareholder approval or satisfy other closing conditions; (4)&#160;the inability to complete the Private Placement Transactions, (5)&#160;changes to the structure, timing, or terms of the Proposed Transactions; (6)&#160;the ability of the combined company to meet applicable listing standards or to maintain the listing of its securities following the closing of the Business Combination; (7)&#160;the risk that the announcement and consummation of the transaction disrupts current plans and operations; (8)&#160;the ability to recognize the anticipated benefits of the Business Combination, including the ability to build and manage an institutional XRP treasury, execute DeFi yield strategies, and drive institutional adoption of XRP; (9)&#160;changes in market, regulatory, political, and economic conditions affecting digital assets generally or XRP specifically; (10)&#160;the costs related to the Proposed Transactions and those arising as a result of becoming a public company; (11)&#160;the level of redemptions of SPAC&#8217;s public shareholders which may reduce the public float of, reduce the liquidity of the trading market of, and/or maintain the quotation, listing, or trading of securities of SPAC or of Pubco; (12)&#160;the volatility of the price of XRP and other digital assets, the correlation between XRP&#8217;s price and the value of Pubco&#8217;s securities, and the risk that the price of XRP may decrease between the signing of the definitive documents for the Proposed Transactions and the closing of the Proposed Transactions or at any time after the closing of the Proposed Transactions; (13)&#160;risks related to increased competition in the industries in which Pubco will operate; (14)&#160;risks related to changes in U.S. or foreign laws and regulations applicable to digital assets or securities; (15)&#160;the possibility that the combined company may be adversely affected by competitive factors, investor sentiment, or other macroeconomic conditions; (16)&#160;the risk of being considered to be a &#8220;shell company&#8221; by any stock exchange on which the Pubco securities will be listed or by the SEC, which may impact the ability to list Pubco&#8217;s securities and restrict reliance on certain rules or forms in connection with the offering, sale or resale of securities; (17)&#160;the outcome of any potential legal proceedings that may be instituted against the Company, SPAC, Pubco or others following announcement of the Business Combination; and (18)&#160;other risks detailed from time to time in SPAC&#8217;s filings with the SEC, including the Registration Statement and related documents filed or to be filed in connection with the Business Combination. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; You should carefully consider the foregoing factors and the other risks and uncertainties described in the &#8220;Risk Factors&#8221; section of the final prospectus of SPAC dated May&#160;20, 2025 and filed by SPAC with the SEC on May&#160;21, 2025, SPAC&#8217;s Quarterly Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-Q</span> filed with the SEC on August&#160;11, 2025, and the Registration Statement and Proxy Statement/Prospectus that will be filed by Pubco and SPAC, and other documents filed by SPAC and Pubco from time to time with the SEC, as well as the list of risk factors included herein. These filings do or will identify and address other important risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from those contained in the forward-looking statements.  <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE" STYLE="line-height:Normal">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Armada Acquisition Corp. II Announces Ticker Symbol to Change to XRPN on Oct 30, 2025 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>New Ticker Aligns with new $1&nbsp;billion strategy for XRP exposure on NASDAQ </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">MIAMI, FL, Oct. 29, 2025 (PRNewswire) &#8211; Armada Acquisition Corp. II, a special purpose acquisition company (&#8220;Armada II&#8221;)
sponsored by <U>Arrington XRP Capital</U> Fund, today announced that it will change the ticker symbol for its Class&nbsp;A ordinary shares on NASDAQ from &#8220;AACI&#8221; to &#8220;XRPN&#8221;. In addition, the ticker symbol for its units will
change from &#8220;AACIU&#8221; to &#8220;XRPNU&#8221; and the ticker symbol for its warrants will change from &#8220;AACIW&#8221; to &#8220;XRPNW&#8221;. The ticker symbol changes will be effective upon the commencement of trading on NASDAQ on
October&nbsp;30, 2025. Representing a key milestone in the company&#8217;s strategic transformation, this change underscores the company&#8217;s evolution into the world&#8217;s leading institutional XRP digital asset treasury company. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The ticker symbol changes come on the heels of last week&#8217;s <U>announcement</U> that Evernorth Holdings, Inc., a newly formed Nevada
corporation (&#8220;Evernorth&#8221;), has executed a business combination agreement with Armada II (the &#8220;Business Combination Agreement&#8221;) which will result in a new company that has raised over $1&nbsp;billion in gross proceeds to fund
open-market purchases of XRP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">&#8220;As the SPAC sponsor and longtime XRP fanatics, we at Arrington Capital have high conviction in
Evernorth&#8217;s ability to drive meaningful impact and add shareholder value,&#8221; said Michael Arrington, founder of Arrington Capital&nbsp;&amp; Chairman of the Board at Armada Acquisition Corp. II. &#8220;In recent months, XRP has maintained
its prominence in an ecosystem that continues to expand through bold product innovations, a relentless community and a string of notable new contributors&#8212;including Hidden Road, GTreasury, Rail and Standard Custody.&#8221; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">For more information on Evernorth, visit <U>www.evernorth.xyz</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Evernorth </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">At closing of a newly
announced Business Combination Agreement with Armada II, Evernorth will be a publicly traded digital asset treasury that provides investors with exposure to XRP through a regulated, liquid, and transparent structure. Unlike ETFs, Evernorth intends
to actively grow its XRP per share through a mix of institutional and DeFi yield strategies, ecosystem participation, and capital markets activities. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>About Arrington Capital </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Arrington Capital is a digital asset management firm primarily focused on blockchain-based capital markets. The firm, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-founded</FONT> in 2017 by TechCrunch and CrunchBase founder Michael Arrington, has invested in hundreds of startups around the world. Arrington Capital is a seasoned, international team composed of Silicon Valley
veterans and operators with deep venture capital experience and crypto native roots. Arrington XRP Capital Fund, LP is the SPAC sponsor for Armada Acquisition Corp II Additionally, Rippleworks&#8217; investment in this PIPE transaction will be done
through the Arrington XRP Capital Fund, LP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>About Armada Acquisition Corp. II (Nasdaq: XRPN) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Armada II is a special purpose acquisition company formed for the purpose of effecting a merger, share exchange, asset acquisition, share
purchase, recapitalization, reorganization or similar business combination with one or more businesses. Armada II was founded on October&nbsp;3, 2024. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B><I>Additional Information and Where to Find It </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Armada II and Evernorth intend to file with the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;SEC&#8221;) a Registration Statement on Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-4</FONT> (as may be amended, the &#8220;Registration Statement&#8221;), which will include a preliminary proxy statement of Armada II and a prospectus of Evernorth (the &#8220;Proxy Statement/Prospectus&#8221;) in
connection with the proposed business combination (the &#8220;Business Combination&#8221;), certain private placements of securities in connection with the Business Combination (the &#8220;Private Placement Transactions&#8221;) and the other
transactions contemplated by the Business Combination Agreement and/or as described in this press release (together with the Business Combination and the Private Placement Transactions, the &#8220;Proposed Transactions&#8221;). The definitive proxy
statement and other relevant documents will be mailed to shareholders of Armada II as of the record date to be established for voting on the Business Combination and other matters as described in the Proxy Statement/Prospectus. Armada II and/or
Evernorth will also file other documents regarding the Proposed Transactions with the SEC. This press release does not contain all of the information that should be considered concerning the Proposed Transactions and is not intended to form the
basis of any investment decision or any other decision in respect of the Proposed Transactions. BEFORE MAKING ANY VOTING OR INVESTMENT DECISION, SHAREHOLDERS OF ARMADA II AND OTHER INTERESTED PARTIES ARE URGED TO READ, WHEN AVAILABLE, THE
PRELIMINARY PROXY STATEMENT/PROSPECTUS, AND AMENDMENTS THERETO, AND THE DEFINITIVE PROXY STATEMENT/PROSPECTUS AND ALL OTHER RELEVANT DOCUMENTS FILED OR THAT WILL BE FILED WITH THE SEC IN CONNECTION WITH ARMADA II&#8217;S SOLICITATION OF PROXIES FOR
THE EXTRAORDINARY GENERAL MEETING OF ITS SHAREHOLDERS TO BE HELD TO APPROVE THE PROPOSED TRANSACTIONS AND OTHER MATTERS AS DESCRIBED IN THE PROXY STATEMENT/PROSPECTUS BECAUSE THESE DOCUMENTS WILL CONTAIN IMPORTANT INFORMATION ABOUT ARMADA II,
PATHFINDER DIGITAL ASSETS LLC, EVERNORTH AND THE PROPOSED TRANSACTIONS. Investors and security holders will also be able to obtain copies of the Registration Statement and the Proxy Statement/Prospectus and all other documents filed or to be filed
with the SEC by Armada II and Evernorth, without charge, once available, on the SEC&#8217;s website at www.sec.gov, or by directing a request to: Armada Acquisition Corp. II, 382 NE 191st St., Suite 52895, Miami, Florida 33179-52895; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-mail:</FONT> finance@arringtoncapital.com, or to: Evernorth Holdings Inc., 600 Battery St, San Francisco, CA 94111, email: finance@evernorth.xyz. </P>
</DIV></Center>
